From the edge of the Primm fashion outlet mall, I realized that I could wander out into the adjacent desert, and so I did. Habitat was dominated by low sage and creosote scrub, crisscrossed by various unpaved tracks. I first walked southwest, from the southern border of the mall, along a dirt road, which apparently put me in San Bernardino County, California. I then turned back east and wandered along the southern and southeastern edges of a sewage treatment plant, the basins of which were dry (and so this plant probably no longer is in service). From here I continued farther east, reaching a railway line. I walked a short distance north along the tracks, then returned back to the sewage treatment plant and the perimeter of the outlet mall. Wednesday. Civil twilight begins 06:22; sunrise 06:51; sunset 16:45; civil twilight ends 17:02 (these data for Las Vegas). Pacific Standard Time.
